# Test Report

Time: 2024-03-30 07:33:55.384301

### Base Program

```py
def constructArray(n: int, k: int) -> List[int]:
    answer = [0] * n
    for i in range(n):
        if i % 2 == 0:
            answer[i] = i // 2 + 1
        else:
            answer[i] = n - (i - 1) // 2
            k -= 1
    if k > 0:
        for i in range(n - 2, -1, -1):
            if k > 0:
                answer[i] = answer[i + 1] - answer[i]
                k -= 1
    return answer
```

## Test Case 1

### Modified Program

```py

def constructArray(n: int, k: int) -> List[int]:
    answer = [0] * n
    for i in range(n):
        if i % 2 == 0:
            answer[i] = i // 2 + 1
        else:
            answer[i] = n - (i - 1) // 2
            k -= 1
    if k > 0:
        for i in range(n - 2, -1, -1):
            if k > 0:
                answer[i] = answer[i + 1] - answer[i]
                k -= 1
    return answer


```

## Test Case 2

### Modified Program

```py

def constructArray(n: int, k: int) -> List[int]:
    answer = [0] * n
    for i in range(n):
        if i % 2 == 0:
            answer[i] = i // 2 + 1
        else:
            answer[i] = n - (i - 1) // 2
            k -= 1
    if k > 0:
        for i in range(n - 2, -1, -1):
            if k > 0:
                answer[i] = answer[i + 1] - answer[i]
                k -= 1
    return answer


```

## Test Case 3

### Modified Program

```py

def constructArray(n: int, k: int) -> List[int]:
    answer = [0] * n
    for i in range(n):
        if i % 2 == 0:
            answer[i] = i // 2 + 1
        else:
            answer[i] = n - (i - 1) // 2
            k -= 1
    if k > 0:
        for i in range(n - 2, -1, -1):
            if k > 0:
                answer[i] = answer[i + 1] - answer[i]
                k -= 1
    return answer


```

## Test Case 4

### Modified Program

```py

def constructArray(n: int, k: int) -> List[int]:
    answer = [0] * n
    for i in range(n):
        if i % 2 == 0:
            answer[i] = i // 2 + 1
        else:
            answer[i] = n - (i - 1) // 2
            k -= 1
    if k > 0:
        for i in range(n - 2, -1, -1):
            if k > 0:
                answer[i] = answer[i + 1] - answer[i]
                k -= 1
    return answer


```

## Test Case 5

### Modified Program

```py

def constructArray(n: int, k: int) -> List[int]:
    answer = [0] * n
    for i in range(n):
        if i % 2 == 0:
            answer[i] = i // 2 + 1
        else:
            answer[i] = n - (i - 1) // 2
            k -= 1
    if k > 0:
        for i in range(n - 2, -1, -1):
            if k > 0:
                answer[i] = answer[i + 1] - answer[i]
                k -= 1
    return answer


```

## Test Case 6

### Modified Program

```py

def constructArray(n: int, k: int) -> List[int]:
    answer = [0] * n
    for i in range(n):
        if i % 2 == 0:
            answer[i] = i // 2 + 1
        else:
            answer[i] = n - (i - 1) // 2
            k -= 1
    if k > 0:
        for i in range(n - 2, -1, -1):
            if k > 0:
                answer[i] = answer[i + 1] - answer[i]
                k -= 1
    return answer


```

## Test Case 7

### Modified Program

```py

def constructArray(n: int, k: int) -> List[int]:
    answer = [0] * n
    for i in range(n):
        if i % 2 == 0:
            answer[i] = i // 2 + 1
        else:
            answer[i] = n - (i - 1) // 2
            k -= 1
    if k > 0:
        for i in range(n - 2, -1, -1):
            if k > 0:
                answer[i] = answer[i + 1] - answer[i]
                k -= 1
    return answer


```

## Test Case 8

### Modified Program

```py

def constructArray(n: int, k: int) -> List[int]:
    answer = [0] * n
    for i in range(n):
        if i % 2 == 0:
            answer[i] = i // 2 + 1
        else:
            answer[i] = n - (i - 1) // 2
            k -= 1
    if k > 0:
        for i in range(n - 2, -1, -1):
            if k > 0:
                answer[i] = answer[i + 1] - answer[i]
                k -= 1
    return answer


```

## Test Case 9

### Modified Program

```py

def constructArray(n: int, k: int) -> List[int]:
    answer = [0] * n
    for i in range(n):
        if i % 2 == 0:
            answer[i] = i // 2 + 1
        else:
            answer[i] = n - (i - 1) // 2
            k -= 1
    if k > 0:
        for i in range(n - 2, -1, -1):
            if k > 0:
                answer[i] = answer[i + 1] - answer[i]
                k -= 1
    return answer


```

## Test Case 10

### Modified Program

```py

def constructArray(n: int, k: int) -> List[int]:
    answer = [0] * n
    for i in range(n):
        if i % 2 == 0:
            answer[i] = i // 2 + 1
        else:
            answer[i] = n - (i - 1) // 2
            k -= 1
    if k > 0:
        for i in range(n - 2, -1, -1):
            if k > 0:
                answer[i] = answer[i + 1] - answer[i]
                k -= 1
    return answer


```
